### Military Focuses ###

shared_focus = {
	id = ANG_army_stuff
	icon = GFX_focus_ger_oppose_hitler
	cost = 5.80
	ai_will_do = { factor = 80 }
	x = 19
	y = 0
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ANG_army_stuff"
		army_experience = 15
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = ANG_mass_combat
	icon = GFX_goal_conscription
	x = -2
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = ANG_army_stuff
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_army_stuff }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = ANG_trenches }
	mutually_exclusive = { focus = ANG_massive_firepower }

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 80
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_tech = superior_firepower
				has_tech = mobile_warfare
				has_tech = trench_warfare
				is_researching_technology = superior_firepower
				is_researching_technology = mobile_warfare
				is_researching_technology = trench_warfare
			}
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ANG_mass_combat"
		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = cat_mass_assault
			bonus = 1.0
			uses = 2
			category = cat_mass_assault
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = ANG_filled_arsenals
	icon = GFX_goal_munitions_factories
	x = -3
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = ANG_army_stuff
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_modern_infantry }
	available = {
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
			free_building_slots = {
				building = arms_factory
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 80
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ANG_filled_arsenals"
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = 900 producer = GRI }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment amount = 300 producer = GRI }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment amount = 150 producer = GRI }
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = ANG_fighter_projects
	icon = GFX_goal_generic_air_fighter
	x = -2
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = ANG_air_stuff
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_air_stuff }

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 30
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ANG_fighter_projects"
		if = {
			limit = {
			    has_tech = early_fighter
		    }
		    add_tech_bonus = {
				name = fighter_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 1
				technology = fighter1
				technology = fighter2
				technology = fighter3
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = fighter_equipment
				amount = 50
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_technology = {
				early_fighter = 1
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = fighter_equipment
				amount = 50
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = ANG_angriver_forever
	icon = GFX_goal_munitions_factories
	x = -2
	y = 8
	relative_position_id = ANG_the_marshals_takeover
	cost = 5.80

		has_government = democratic
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
			free_building_slots = {
				building = arms_factory
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ANG_angriver_forever"
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = arms_factory
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = arms_factory
									size > 0

	}

								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

	id = ANG_into_the_factories

	x = 2

	relative_position_id = ANG_heartless_creatures

		has_government = fascism
		any_owned_state = {
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
			free_building_slots = {
				building = industrial_complex
				size > 0
				include_locked = yes
			}
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}

			limit = {

					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex
									size > 0
									include_locked = yes
								}
								is_in_home_area = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
				OR = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							any_owned_state = {
								free_building_slots = {
									building = industrial_complex

	id = ANG_the_congress
	icon = GFX_goal_HOL_council_communism
	x = 0
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = ANG_the_commune
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_take_feathisia_greiffenheim }
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_take_bronzehill_strawberry }
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_take_romau_and_yale }
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_take_katerin }
	available = {
		has_government = communism
		OR = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } STW = { exists = no } }
		OR = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } FEA = { exists = no } }
		OR = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } BRZ = { exists = no } }
		OR = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } KAT = { exists = no } }
		OR = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ROU = { exists = no } }
		OR = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } YAL = { exists = no } }
		OR = { PYT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } PYT = { exists = no } }
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ANG_the_congress"
		custom_effect_tooltip = ANG_heartland_cores_tp
		set_global_flag = GRI_empire_rising_flag
		country_event = { id = angriver.50 days = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						is_core_of = FEA
						is_core_of = STW
						is_core_of = PYT
						is_core_of = BRZ
						is_core_of = KAT
						is_core_of = YAL
						is_core_of = ROU
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = FEA transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = BRZ transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = KAT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ROU transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = YAL transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { PYT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PYT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = STW transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = ANG_expand_the_army
	icon = GFX_goal_officers
	x = 3
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = ANG_the_protege
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_guardians_of_the_constitution }
	available = {
		OR = {
			has_government = democratic
			has_government = neutrality
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ANG_expand_the_army"
		add_manpower = 10000
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = disarmed_nation }
			add_ideas = volunteer_only
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = volunteer_only }
			add_ideas = limited_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = limited_conscription }
			add_ideas = extensive_conscription
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = extensive_conscription }
			add_ideas = service_by_requirement
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = service_by_requirement }
			add_ideas = all_adults_serve
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = all_adults_serve }
			add_ideas = scraping_the_barrel
		}
	}
}

	id = ANG_the_new_state
	icon = GFX_goal_ideology_national_populist
	x = 0
	y = 3
	relative_position_id = ANG_be_ready
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_take_feathisia_greiffenheim_claw }
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_take_bronzehill_strawberry_claw }
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_take_romau_and_yale_claw }
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_take_katerin_claw }

	available = {
		OR = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } STW = { exists = no } }
		OR = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } FEA = { exists = no } }
		OR = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } BRZ = { exists = no } }
		OR = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } KAT = { exists = no } }
		OR = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } ROU = { exists = no } }
		OR = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } YAL = { exists = no } }
		OR = { PYT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } PYT = { exists = no } }
		has_government = fascism
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ANG_the_new_state"
		custom_effect_tooltip = ANG_heartland_cores_tp
		set_global_flag = GRI_empire_rising_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						is_core_of = FEA
						is_core_of = STW
						is_core_of = PYT
						is_core_of = BRZ
						is_core_of = KAT
						is_core_of = YAL
						is_core_of = ROU
					}
				}
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { FEA = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = FEA transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = BRZ transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KAT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = KAT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ROU = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = ROU transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { YAL = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = YAL transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { PYT = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PYT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { STW = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = STW transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
}

				limit = { 
					OR = {
						is_core_of = FEA
						is_core_of = STW

						is_core_of = BRZ

						is_core_of = YAL

					}

			}

				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = FEA transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = BRZ transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {

				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = KAT transfer_troops = yes } }
			}
			if = {

			}

			}
			if = {

				limit = { BRZ = { is_subject_of = ROOT } }
				ROOT = { annex_country = { target = BRZ transfer_troops = yes } }

shared_focus = {
	id = ANG_reclaim_nova_griffonia
	icon = GFX_goal_authority
	x = 0
	y = 7
	relative_position_id = ANG_the_god_emperor
	cost = 5.80
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_core_south_baron }
	prerequisite = { focus = ANG_core_frontier_baron }
	available = {
		has_government = fascism
		is_subject = no
		any_owned_state = {
			is_coastal = yes
		}
	}
	bypass = {
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GRF
			has_war_with = GFF
		}
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 100
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_war = yes
		}
	}
	will_lead_to_war_with = GRF
	will_lead_to_war_with = GFF
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ANG_reclaim_nova_griffonia"
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GRF }
			GRF = { country_event = { id = imperial.61 days = 7 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { GFF = { exists = yes is_subject = no } }
			GFF = { country_event = { id = imperial.61 days = 7 } }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = { is_core_of = GRF is_core_of = GFF }
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
}
